    if (typeof window.rdmEnableRaygunCrashReporting !== "boolean") window.rdmEnableRaygunCrashReporting = true;
    if (typeof window.rdmEnableRaygunPulse !== "boolean") window.rdmEnableRaygunPulse = false;

    var additionalTags = typeof window.rdmRaygunTags === "function"
        ? window.rdmRaygunTags()
        : window.rdmRaygunTags;

    var tags = Array.isArray(additionalTags)
